Computes the plane given three points(clockwise). 

Calculates the plane given three points(clockwise) by taking the perpendicular vector that would intersect a triangle that the three points represent. The plane is defined as a normal and distance from the origin. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur when the given plane\textquotesingle{}s position points are collinear.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+plane\+PositionA} & The plane position a. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+plane\+PositionB} & The plane position b. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+plane\+PositionC} & The plane position c. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Plane} & The out plane.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Tests whether a triangle is non-\/degenerate. 

Tests whether a triangle is non-\/degenerate. A non-\/degenerate triangle has an area greater than 0 and is not a line. If the triangle is non-\/degenerate, the out result is 1. If the triangle is degenerate, the out result is 0.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TestPointToConvexPolygonF()}{TestPointToConvexPolygonF()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Point\+To\+Convex\+PolygonF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}}}]{\+\_\+point,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+polygon\+Points,  }\item[{const unsigned int}]{\+\_\+points\+Count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Tests whether a point lies within a polygon or not. 

Tests whether a point is contained within a polygon by counting how many times a line that extends to infinity intersects the sides of the polygon. If the point is contained within the polygon, the out result is 1. This does not include the polygon\textquotesingle{}s boundary. If the point is not contained within the polygon, the out result is 0. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the pointer to the polygon\textquotesingle{}s points is null or if the point count is less than 3.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+point} & The query point. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+polygon\+Points} & If non-\/null, the set of points representing the polygon vertices. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+points\+Count} & The number of polygon vertices. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Result} & The out result.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Computes the closest points of two lines. 

Computes the closest points of two lines by determining the minimum distance that could exist between the two line segments which results in the two closest points from one line to the other. The first out point is the point closest to the second line clamped to the first line. The second out point is the point closest to the first line clamped to the second line.

Computes the closest point on a plane to a point. 

Computes the closest point on a plane to a point by projecting that point onto the plane. The out point is the result of this computation.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Closest\+Point\+To\+SphereF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_s_p_h_e_r_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+S\+P\+H\+E\+R\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+sphere,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}}}]{\+\_\+query\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Point }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Computes the closest point on a sphere\textquotesingle{}s surface to a point. 

Computes the closest point on a sphere\textquotesingle{}s surface to a point by getting the normalized direction of the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center to the given point and scaling that by the sphere\textquotesingle{}s radius. The out point is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the query point is the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center which results an infinite amount of valid results that cannot be represented in a single out point.

\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+sphere} & The sphere. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+query\+Point} & The query point. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Point} & The out point that lies on the sphere\textquotesingle{}s surface.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Closest\+Point\+To\+CapsuleF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_c_a_p_s_u_l_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+L\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+capsule,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}}}]{\+\_\+query\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Point }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Computes the closest point on a capsule\textquotesingle{}s surface to a point. 

Computes the closest point on a capsule\textquotesingle{}s surface to a point by finding the closest point to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and then computing the closest point to a sphere. The out point is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the query point is on the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line which results an infinite amount of valid results that cannot be represented in a single out point.

Computes the closest point on a min-\/max A\+A\+BB to a point. 

Computes the closest point on a min-\/max A\+A\+BB to a point by clamping that point to the surface of the A\+A\+BB unless that point is contained within the A\+A\+BB. The out point is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the query point is contained within the A\+A\+BB.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Compute\+Sphere\+From\+PointsF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+point\+Cloud,  }\item[{const unsigned int}]{\+\_\+points\+Count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_s_p_h_e_r_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+S\+P\+H\+E\+R\+EF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Sphere }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Compute sphere from point cloud. 

Computes a sphere from a point cloud by computing a good approximation of the points in the sphere and then iterating through the points to grow the sphere to include all points. The out sphere is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the pointer to the point cloud is N\+U\+LL or the number of points is less than 2.

Compute min-\/max A\+A\+BB from point cloud. 

Computes a min-\/max A\+A\+BB from point cloud by computing the minimum and maximum values along the x, y, and z from the point cloud. The out A\+A\+BB is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the pointer to the point cloud is N\+U\+LL or the number of points is less than 1.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Point\+To\+TriangleF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}}}]{\+\_\+point,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+triangle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Test a point to triangle. 

Tests a point to a triangle by checking if the point lies on the surface plane of the triangle\textquotesingle{}s normal and then if the barycentric coordinate\textquotesingle{}s are all positive. If the point lies on the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the point does not lie on the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the triangle is degenerate.

Test a point to a plane. 

Tests a point to a plane by dotting the point and the plane\textquotesingle{}s surface direction and then subtracting the plane\textquotesingle{}s distance from the result of that dot product. If the point lies on the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the point lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the point lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a line to a line. 

Test a line to a line by computing the shortest distance between the lines. If the first line contacts the second line, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the first line does not contact the second line, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Line\+To\+TriangleF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_l_i_n_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+L\+I\+N\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+line,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+triangle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Test a line to a triangle. 

Test a line to a clockwise triangle by computing if the line pierces the triangle. A collision will only be detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line\textquotesingle{}s start point lies in front of the triangle and the line\textquotesingle{}s end lies in back of the triangle). If the line contacts the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line does not contact the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+triangle} & The triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Result} & The out result. \\
\hline

Test a line to a plane. 

Test a line to a plane by computing the interval along the line that intersects the plane. If the line contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the line lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a line to an O\+BB by checking if any section of the line lies within the O\+BB\textquotesingle{}s bounds. If the line contacts the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. Test a ray to a triangle. 

Test a ray to a clockwise triangle by computing if the ray\textquotesingle{}s path intersects the triangle. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.

Test a ray to a plane. 

Test a ray to a plane by computing if the ray\textquotesingle{}s path pierces the plane. If the ray contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the ray lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a ray to a sphere. 

Tests if a collision exists between ray to sphere by using the quadratic formula to determine if there are any points of intersection (roots). If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a ray to a capsule. 

Test a ray to a capsule by computing the closest points on the ray\textquotesingle{}s path to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and reduces the query to a point to sphere test. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Triangle\+To\+TriangleF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+triangle1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+triangle2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Test a triangle to a triangle. 

Test a triangle to a triangle by first checking if all either triangle\textquotesingle{}s point lie on one side of the other triangle\textquotesingle{}s face and then brings the triangles into canonical form to check if any of the edges of one triangle intersect the other triangle. If the triangle\textquotesingle{}s contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle\textquotesingle{}s don\textquotesingle{}t contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

\hline

\hline

Test a triangle to a plane. 

Test a triangle to a plane to compute if all of the triangle\textquotesingle{}s vertices lie completely on one side of the plane. If the triangle contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the triangle lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a triangle to a sphere. 

Test a triangle to a sphere by computing the closest point on the triangle to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center which reduces the query to testing a point to sphere. If the triangle contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle is coplanar to the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a triangle to a capsule. 

Test a triangle to capsule by computing a line on the triangle closest to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line which reduces the query to test a line to capsule. If the triangle contacts the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle does not contact the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Triangle\+To\+A\+A\+B\+BF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+triangle,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_a_a_b_b_c_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+A\+A\+B\+B\+C\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+aabb,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Test a triangle to an A\+A\+BB. 

Test a triangle to A\+A\+BB by using the separating axis theorem which involves 13 axis\+: 3 face normals of the A\+A\+BB, 1 face normal of the triangle, 9 cross products between the their edges. If the triangle contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle does not contact the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a triangle to an O\+BB. 

Test a triangle to an O\+BB by bringing the triangle into the O\+BB\textquotesingle{}s space and performing a triangle to A\+A\+BB test. If the triangle contacts the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. Test a plane to a sphere. 

Test a plane to a sphere by computing the closest point on the plane to the sphere and perform a point to sphere test. If the plane contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the sphere lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the sphere lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a plane to a capsule. 

Test a plane to a capsule by computing the closest points on the plane to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s start and end points and then perform a line to capsule test. If the plane contacts the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. Test a plane to an A\+A\+BB.

If the plane contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. Test a sphere to sphere.

If the spheres contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. Test a sphere to an A\+A\+BB. 

Test a sphere to an A\+A\+BB by computing the distance from the A\+A\+BB\textquotesingle{}s boundary to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center and computing if that distance is within the sphere\textquotesingle{}s radius. If the sphere contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the sphere does not contact the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a sphere to an O\+BB. 

Test a sphere to an O\+BB by computing the distance from the O\+BB\textquotesingle{}s boundary to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center and computing if that distance is within the sphere\textquotesingle{}s radius. If the sphere contacts the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the sphere does not contact the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TestOBBToOBBF()}{TestOBBToOBBF()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+O\+B\+B\+To\+O\+B\+BF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_o_b_b_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+O\+B\+BF}}}]{\+\_\+obb1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_o_b_b_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+O\+B\+BF}}}]{\+\_\+obb2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Tests O\+BB to O\+BB. 

Tests if a collision exists between O\+BB to O\+BB by checking if the sum of their projected radii is less than the distance between their projected centers meaning a separating axis exists. The result will be stored in \+\_\+out\+Result as either \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the O\+B\+Bs contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the O\+B\+Bs don\textquotesingle{}t contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Intersect\+Line\+To\+TriangleF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_l_i_n_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+L\+I\+N\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+line,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+triangle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Direction,  }\item[{float \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Interval }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect line to triangle. 

Test a line to a clockwise triangle by computing if the line pierces the triangle. A collision will only be detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line\textquotesingle{}s start point lies in front of the triangle and the line\textquotesingle{}s end lies in back of the triangle). Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line does not contact the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.

Intersect line to plane. 

Test a line to a plane by computing the interval along the line that intersects the plane. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the line lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Intersect line to sphere.

Intersect line to capsule.

Intersect line to A\+A\+BB. 

Test a line to an A\+A\+BB by checking if any section of the line lies within the A\+A\+BB\textquotesingle{}s bounds. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line does not contact the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur when the line degenerates to a point.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{IntersectLineToOBBF()}{IntersectLineToOBBF()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Intersect\+Line\+To\+O\+B\+BF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_l_i_n_e_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+L\+I\+N\+EF}}}]{\+\_\+line,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_o_b_b_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+O\+B\+BF}}}]{\+\_\+obb,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Direction,  }\item[{float \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Interval }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect line to O\+BB. 

Test a line to an O\+BB by checking if any section of the line lies within the O\+BB\textquotesingle{}s bounds. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line does not contact the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur when the line degenerates to a point.

Intersect ray to triangle. 

Test a ray to a clockwise triangle by computing if the ray\textquotesingle{}s path intersects the triangle. Provides the point of contact along with the interval the contact occurs on the ray. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.

Intersect ray to plane. 

Test a ray to a plane by computing if the ray\textquotesingle{}s path pierces the plane. Provides the point of contact along with the interval the contact occurs on the ray. If the ray contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the ray lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Intersect ray to sphere. 

Tests if a collision exists between ray to sphere by using the quadratic formula to determine if there are any points of intersection (roots). Provides the point of contact along with the interval the contact occurs on the ray. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Intersect ray to capsule. 

Test a ray to a capsule by computing the closest points on the ray\textquotesingle{}s path to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and reduces the query to a point to sphere test. {\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Intersect\+Ray\+To\+O\+B\+BF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_r_a_y_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+R\+A\+YF}}}]{\+\_\+ray,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_o_b_b_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+O\+B\+BF}}}]{\+\_\+obb,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point,  }\item[{float \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Interval }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect ray to O\+BB. 

Test a ray to an O\+BB by checking if any section of the ray\textquotesingle{}s path lies within the A\+A\+BB\textquotesingle{}s bounds. Provides the point of contact along with the interval the contact occurs on the ray. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Intersect sphere to sphere. 

Test a sphere to sphere by checking the distance between their centers and the sum of their radii. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the spheres contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the spheres do not contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline

\hline

Intersect sphere to capsule. 

Test a sphere to capsule by checking the distance between each\textquotesingle{}s center structures and the sum of their radii. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. Intersect sphere to A\+A\+BB. 

Test a sphere to an A\+A\+BB by computing the distance from the A\+A\+BB\textquotesingle{}s boundary to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center and computing if that distance is within the sphere\textquotesingle{}s radius. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the sphere contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the sphere does not contact the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Intersect capsule to capsule. 

Test a capsule to another capsule by computing the closest points on each capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and performing a sphere to sphere test. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the capsules contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the capsules don\textquotesingle{}t contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Intersect capsule to A\+A\+BB. 

Test a capsule to an A\+A\+BB by increasing the A\+A\+BB\textquotesingle{}s extents by the capsule\textquotesingle{}s radius and then performing a ray to A\+A\+BB test. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the capsule contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the capsule does not contact the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Intersect capsule to O\+BB. 

Test a capsule to an O\+BB by bringing the capsule into the O\+BB\textquotesingle{}s space and performing a capsule to A\+A\+BB test. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the capsule contacts the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the capsule does not contact the O\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Intersect A\+A\+BB to A\+A\+BB. 

Test an A\+A\+BB to an A\+A\+BB by checking if they overlap on all three axes. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface,the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the A\+A\+B\+Bs contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the A\+A\+B\+Bs don\textquotesingle{}t contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+BarycentricF (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}}}]{\+\_\+a,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}}}]{\+\_\+b,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}}}]{\+\_\+c,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}}}]{\+\_\+p,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_f}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RF}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Compute the barycentric coordinates of a point to triangle. 

Compute the barycentric coordinates given three points of a triangle with a point in respect to that triangle. Both triangle and point must be coplanar. The result is stored in a vector representing the barycentric coords. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur when the triangle is degenerate.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+a} & The first point of a triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+b} & The second point of a triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+c} & The third point of a triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+p} & The point coplanar with the triangle points. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Barycentric} & The out barycentric coordinates.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Compute\+PlaneD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}}}]{\+\_\+plane\+PositionA,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}}}]{\+\_\+plane\+PositionB,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}}}]{\+\_\+plane\+PositionC,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_p_l_a_n_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+P\+L\+A\+N\+ED}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Plane }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Computes the plane given three points(clockwise). 

Calculates the plane given three points(clockwise) by taking the perpendicular vector that would intersect a triangle that the three points represent. The plane is defined as a normal and distance from the origin. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur when the given plane\textquotesingle{}s position points are collinear.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+plane\+PositionC} & The plane position c. \\
\hline

Tests whether a triangle is non-\/degenerate. 

Tests whether a triangle is non-\/degenerate. A non-\/degenerate triangle has an area greater than 0 and is not a line. If the triangle is non-\/degenerate, the out result is 1. If the triangle is degenerate, the out result is 0.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Point\+To\+Convex\+PolygonD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}}}]{\+\_\+point,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+polygon\+Points,  }\item[{const unsigned int}]{\+\_\+points\+Count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Tests whether a point lies within a polygon or not. 

Tests whether a point is contained within a polygon by counting how many times a line that extends to infinity intersects the sides of the polygon. If the point is contained within the polygon, the out result is 1. This does not include the polygon\textquotesingle{}s boundary. If the point is not contained within the polygon, the out result is 0. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the pointer to the polygon\textquotesingle{}s points is null or if the point count is less than 3.

\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+point} & The query point. \\
\hline

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+points\+Count} & The number of polygon vertices. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Result} & The out result.\\

Computes the closest points of two lines. 

Computes the closest points of two lines by determining the minimum distance that could exist between the two line segments which results in the two closest points from one line to the other. The first out point is the point closest to the second line clamped to the first line. The second out point is the point closest to the first line clamped to the second line.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Closest\+Point\+To\+SphereD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_s_p_h_e_r_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+S\+P\+H\+E\+R\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+sphere,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}}}]{\+\_\+query\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Point }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Computes the closest point on a sphere\textquotesingle{}s surface to a point. 

Computes the closest point on a sphere\textquotesingle{}s surface to a point by getting the normalized direction of the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center to the given point and scaling that by the sphere\textquotesingle{}s radius. The out point is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the query point is the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center which results an infinite amount of valid results that cannot be represented in a single out point.

Computes the closest point on a capsule\textquotesingle{}s surface to a point. 

Computes the closest point on a capsule\textquotesingle{}s surface to a point by finding the closest point to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and then computing the closest point to a sphere. The out point is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the query point is on the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line which results an infinite amount of valid results that cannot be represented in a single out point.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+capsule} & The capsule. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+query\+Point} & The query point. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Point} & The out point that lies on the capsule\textquotesingle{}s surface.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Closest\+Point\+To\+A\+A\+B\+BD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_a_a_b_b_m_m_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+A\+A\+B\+B\+M\+MD}}}]{\+\_\+aabb,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}}}]{\+\_\+query\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Point }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Computes the closest point on a min-\/max A\+A\+BB to a point. 

Computes the closest point on a min-\/max A\+A\+BB to a point by clamping that point to the surface of the A\+A\+BB unless that point is contained within the A\+A\+BB. The out point is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the query point is contained within the A\+A\+BB.

Computes the closest point on an O\+BB to a point. 

Computes the closest point on an O\+BB to a point by clamping that point to the surface of the O\+BB. The out point is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the query point is contained within the O\+BB.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Compute\+Sphere\+From\+PointsD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+point\+Cloud,  }\item[{const unsigned int}]{\+\_\+points\+Count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_s_p_h_e_r_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+S\+P\+H\+E\+R\+ED}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Sphere }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Compute sphere from point cloud. 

Computes a sphere from a point cloud by computing a good approximation of the points in the sphere and then iterating through the points to grow the sphere to include all points. The out sphere is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the pointer to the point cloud is N\+U\+LL or the number of points is less than 2.

\hline

Compute min-\/max A\+A\+BB from point cloud. 

Computes a min-\/max A\+A\+BB from point cloud by computing the minimum and maximum values along the x, y, and z from the point cloud. The out A\+A\+BB is the result of this computation. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the pointer to the point cloud is N\+U\+LL or the number of points is less than 1.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Point\+To\+TriangleD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}}}]{\+\_\+point,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+triangle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Test a point to triangle. 

Tests a point to a triangle by checking if the point lies on the surface plane of the triangle\textquotesingle{}s normal and then if the barycentric coordinate\textquotesingle{}s are all positive. If the point lies on the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the point does not lie on the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it. If the function succeeds, the return value is S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If the function fails, the return value is F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE. This would occur if the triangle is degenerate.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Point\+To\+PlaneD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}}}]{\+\_\+point,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_p_l_a_n_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+P\+L\+A\+N\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+plane,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Test a point to a plane. 

Tests a point to a plane by dotting the point and the plane\textquotesingle{}s surface direction and then subtracting the plane\textquotesingle{}s distance from the result of that dot product. If the point lies on the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the point lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the point lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a point to a sphere. 

Test a point to a sphere by checking if the distance between the point and sphere\textquotesingle{}s center is within the sphere\textquotesingle{}s radius. If the point contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the point does not contact the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a point to a capsule. 

Test a point to a capsule by finding the closest point along the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line segment to the point which reduces the query to a point to sphere test. If the point contacts the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the point does not contact the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a point to a center-\/extent A\+A\+BB. 

Test a point to a center-\/extent A\+A\+BB by checking if it\textquotesingle{}s within the A\+A\+BB\textquotesingle{}s boundaries along the x, y, and z. If the point contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the point does not contact the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+Line\+To\+TriangleD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_l_i_n_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+L\+I\+N\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+line,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+triangle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Test a line to a triangle. 

Test a line to a clockwise triangle by computing if the line pierces the triangle. A collision will only be detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line\textquotesingle{}s start point lies in front of the triangle and the line\textquotesingle{}s end lies in back of the triangle). If the line contacts the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line does not contact the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+triangle} & The triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Result} & The out result. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Barycentric} & If non-\/null, the out barycentric.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Test a line to a plane. 

Test a line to a plane by computing the interval along the line that intersects the plane. If the line contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the line lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a line to a sphere. 

Test a line to a sphere by computing the closest point on that line to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center and reducing the query to a point to sphere check. If the line contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. Test a ray to a plane. 

Test a ray to a plane by computing if the ray\textquotesingle{}s path pierces the plane. If the ray contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the ray lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a ray to a sphere. 

Tests if a collision exists between ray to sphere by using the quadratic formula to determine if there are any points of intersection (roots). If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a ray to a capsule. 

Test a ray to a capsule by computing the closest points on the ray\textquotesingle{}s path to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and reduces the query to a point to sphere test. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a triangle to a triangle. 

Test a triangle to a triangle by first checking if all either triangle\textquotesingle{}s point lie on one side of the other triangle\textquotesingle{}s face and then brings the triangles into canonical form to check if any of the edges of one triangle intersect the other triangle. If the triangle\textquotesingle{}s contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle\textquotesingle{}s don\textquotesingle{}t contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a triangle to a plane. 

Test a triangle to a plane to compute if all of the triangle\textquotesingle{}s vertices lie completely on one side of the plane. If the triangle contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the triangle lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Test a triangle to a sphere. 

Test a triangle to a sphere by computing the closest point on the triangle to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center which reduces the query to testing a point to sphere. If the triangle contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle is coplanar to the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a triangle to a capsule.

Test a triangle to an A\+A\+BB. 

Test a triangle to A\+A\+BB by using the separating axis theorem which involves 13 axis\+: 3 face normals of the A\+A\+BB, 1 face normal of the triangle, 9 cross products between the their edges. If the triangle contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the triangle does not contact the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Test a capsule to an A\+A\+BB. 

Test a capsule to an A\+A\+BB by increasing the A\+A\+BB\textquotesingle{}s extents by the capsule\textquotesingle{}s radius and then performing a ray to A\+A\+BB test. If the capsule contacts the A\+A\+BB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. {\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Test\+O\+B\+B\+To\+O\+B\+BD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_o_b_b_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+O\+B\+BD}}}]{\+\_\+obb1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_o_b_b_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+O\+B\+BD}}}]{\+\_\+obb2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Tests O\+BB to O\+BB. 

Tests if a collision exists between O\+BB to O\+BB by checking if the sum of their projected radii is less than the distance between their projected centers meaning a separating axis exists. The result will be stored in \+\_\+out\+Result as either \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the O\+B\+Bs contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the O\+B\+Bs don\textquotesingle{}t contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{IntersectLineToTriangleD()}{IntersectLineToTriangleD()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Intersect\+Line\+To\+TriangleD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_l_i_n_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+L\+I\+N\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+line,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+L\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+triangle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Direction,  }\item[{double \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Interval }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect line to triangle. 

Test a line to a clockwise triangle by computing if the line pierces the triangle. A collision will only be detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line\textquotesingle{}s start point lies in front of the triangle and the line\textquotesingle{}s end lies in back of the triangle). Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line does not contact the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+line} & The line. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+triangle} & The triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Result} & The out result. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point} & The out contact point. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Barycentric} & If non-\/null, the out barycentric. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Direction} & The out direction. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Interval} & The out interval along the direction.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{G\+Return}} G\+W\+::\+M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+Collision\+::\+Intersect\+Line\+To\+PlaneD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_l_i_n_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+L\+I\+N\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+line,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_p_l_a_n_e_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+P\+L\+A\+N\+ED}}}]{\+\_\+plane,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{G\+Collision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{M\+A\+T\+H\+::\+G\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+RD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Direction,  }\item[{double \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Interval }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect line to plane. 

Test a line to a plane by computing the interval along the line that intersects the plane. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+B\+E\+L\+OW}}. If the line lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+A\+B\+O\+VE}}.

Intersect line to sphere. 

Test a line to a sphere by computing the closest point on that line to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center and reducing the query to a point to sphere check. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}. If the line does not contact the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{G\+Collision\+Check\+::\+N\+O\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+L\+I\+S\+I\+ON}}.

Intersect line to capsule. 

Test a line to a capsule by finding the closest points of the line to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and reducing the query to a point to sphere check. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs.
